<script defer>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const header = document.getElementById('header-full');
    const sticky = document.getElementById('stickyBar');

    if ('IntersectionObserver' in window && header && sticky) {
      const io = new IntersectionObserver(([e]) => {
        const show = !e.isIntersecting; // show after header leaves viewport
        sticky.classList.toggle('show', show);
        sticky.setAttribute('aria-hidden', show ? 'false' : 'true');
      }, { root: null, threshold: 0, rootMargin: '0px' });

      sticky.classList.remove('show'); // ensure hidden on load
      sticky.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      io.observe(header);
    }
  });

  // Date text is server-rendered; no client formatting needed
</script>

<script>
/* ====== helpers: контекст и безопасный track ====== */
(function () {
  const AMP_QUEUE_KEY = '__ampQueue';
  if (!Array.isArray(window[AMP_QUEUE_KEY])) {
    window[AMP_QUEUE_KEY] = [];
  }

  function flushAmplitudeQueue() {
    const amp = window.amplitude;
    if (!amp || typeof amp.track !== 'function') return;
    const queue = window[AMP_QUEUE_KEY];
    while (queue.length) {
      const item = queue.shift();
      if (!item) continue;
      amp.track(item.eventName, item.props);
    }
  }

  function trackSafe(eventName, props = {}) {
    const amp = window.amplitude;
    if (!amp || typeof amp.track !== 'function') {
      window[AMP_QUEUE_KEY].push({ eventName, props });
      return;
    }
    amp.track(eventName, props); // v2: глобальный amplitude.track
  }

  function getMeta(name) {
    const el = document.querySelector(`meta[data-${name}-label]`);
    return el ? el.getAttribute('content') : '';
  }

  // Текущий контекст фильтров (для присоединения ко всем событиям)
  function ctx() {
    return {
      day_id: (document.querySelector('.filter-link.day.active')?.textContent || '').trim(),
      market_id: (document.querySelector('.filter-link.market.active')?.dataset.market || '').trim(),
      strategy_id: (document.querySelector('.filter-link.strategy.active')?.dataset.mode || '').trim(),
      day_label: getMeta('day') || (document.querySelector('.filter-link.day.active')?.textContent || '').trim(),
      market_label: getMeta('market') || (document.querySelector('.filter-link.market.active')?.textContent || '').trim(),
      strategy_label: getMeta('strategy') || (document.querySelector('.filter-link.strategy.active')?.textContent || '').trim(),
      page_path: location.pathname,
      page_url: location.href
      // page_view автотрекается SDK v2, но эти props полезно прикладывать. :contentReference[oaicite:1]{index=1}
    };
  }

  /* ====== 0) страница загружена (срез наличных матчей) ====== */
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.match-card');
    trackSafe('filters_page_loaded', {
      ...ctx(),
      matches_total: cards.length
    });
  });

  window.addEventListener('amplitude:ready', flushAmplitudeQueue);
  window.addEventListener('load', flushAmplitudeQueue);

  /* ====== 1) клики по фильтрам (Day / Market / Strategy) ====== */
  // Ваша разметка уже имеет .filter-link.{day|market|strategy}
  document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    const a = e.target.closest('a.filter-link');
    if (!a) return;

    const isDay = a.classList.contains('day');
    const isMarket = a.classList.contains('market');
    const isStrategy = a.classList.contains('strategy');

    const filter_type = isDay ? 'day' : isMarket ? 'market' : isStrategy ? 'strategy' : 'other';

    const prev = {
      day_prev: document.querySelector('.filter-link.day.active')?.textContent?.trim() || '',
      market_prev: document.querySelector('.filter-link.market.active')?.dataset.market || '',
      strategy_prev: document.querySelector('.filter-link.strategy.active')?.dataset.mode || ''
    };

    const payload = {
      ...ctx(),
      filter_type,
      filter_value_id: isMarket ? (a.dataset.market || '') : isStrategy ? (a.dataset.mode || '') : (a.textContent || '').trim(),
      filter_value_label: (a.textContent || '').trim(),
      day_prev: prev.day_prev,
      market_prev: prev.market_prev,
      strategy_prev: prev.strategy_prev,
      href: a.href
    };

    trackSafe('filter_change', payload);
  }, true);

  /* ====== 2) показ/скрытие sticky bar (как индикатор продолжения исследования) ====== */
  (function wireStickyIO(){
    const sticky = document.getElementById('stickyBar');
    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
      const visible = sticky.classList.contains('show') ? 'shown' : 'hidden';
      trackSafe('sticky_bar_state', { ...ctx(), state: visible });
    });
    if (sticky) {
      observer.observe(sticky, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['class'] });
    }
  })();

  /* ====== 3) клики по карточке матча ====== */
  // Рекомендуется добавить в .match-card:
  // data-match-id, data-league-slug, data-league-name, data-event-date (ISO), data-has-score
  document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    const card = e.target.closest('.match-card');
    if (!card) return;

    const leagueName = card.querySelector('.league-title')?.textContent?.trim() || '';
    const teams = card.querySelector('.teams')?.textContent?.trim() || '';
    const scoreTag = card.querySelector('.score-tag')?.getAttribute('aria-label') || '';

    trackSafe('match_click', {
      ...ctx(),
      match_id: card.getAttribute('data-match-id') || '',           // ← проставьте в шаблоне
      league_slug: card.getAttribute('data-league-slug') || '',     // ← проставьте в шаблоне
      league_name: card.getAttribute('data-league-name') || leagueName,
      event_date: card.getAttribute('data-event-date') || card.querySelector('time')?.getAttribute('data-event-date') || '',
      has_score: card.getAttribute('data-has-score') || (/\d+\s?:\s?\d+/.test(scoreTag) ? '1' : '0'),
      teams
    });
  }, true);

  /* ====== 4) клики по линиям маркетов (Value pick) ====== */
  // Разметка каждой линии:
  // .market-line внутри .match-card; внутри есть .market-info и .market-edge
  document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    const line = e.target.closest('.market-line');
    if (!line) return;

    const card = e.target.closest('.match-card');
    const market = line.querySelector('.market-info .tag.yellow-tag')?.textContent?.trim() || '';
    const valueStr = line.querySelector('.market-info .tag.blue-tag')?.textContent?.trim() || '';
    const bm = line.querySelector('.market-info .bm')?.textContent?.trim() || '';
    const betValue = line.querySelector('.edge-val.value')?.textContent?.replace('+','').replace('%','').trim() || '';
    const modelProbability = line.querySelector('.edge-prob.blue')?.textContent?.replace('%','').trim() || '';
    const valueClass = line.querySelector('.edge-val.value')?.classList?.contains('high') ? 'high' :
                       line.querySelector('.edge-val.value')?.classList?.contains('mid') ? 'mid' : 'low';

    trackSafe('market_line_click', {
      ...ctx(),
      match_id: card?.getAttribute('data-match-id') || '',
      market,
      pick_value: valueStr,                 // например "O/U 2.5 Over"
      bookmaker_and_odd: bm,                // "Bookmaker · 1.85"
      bet_value_pct: betValue,              // число: "6"
      model_conf_pct: modelProbability,     // число: "58"
      value_bucket: valueClass || ''
    });
  }, true);

  /* ====== 5) scroll depth (25/50/75/100) — чтобы понять, докручивают ли до нужных матчей ====== */
 (function scrollDepth() {
  const marks = new Set();
  let docHeight = 0;
  let ticking = false;

  function updateDocHeight() {
    docHeight = Math.max(
      document.body.scrollHeight,
      document.documentElement.scrollHeight
    );
  }

  function getBucket(p) {
    if (p >= 100) return 100;
    if (p >= 75) return 75;
    if (p >= 50) return 50;
    if (p >= 25) return 25;
    return 0;
  }

  function handleScroll() {
    if (!ticking) {
      ticking = true;
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        const pos = window.scrollY + window.innerHeight;
        const p = Math.min(100, Math.round((pos / docHeight) * 100));
        const bucket = getBucket(p);
        if (bucket && !marks.has(bucket)) {
          marks.add(bucket);
          trackSafe('scroll_depth', { ...ctx(), percent: bucket });
        }
        ticking = false;
      });
    }
  }

  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    updateDocHeight();
    window.addEventListener('resize', updateDocHeight);
    window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll, { passive: true });

    // первый вызов
    const pos = window.scrollY + window.innerHeight;
    const p = Math.min(100, Math.round((pos / docHeight) * 100));
    const bucket = getBucket(p);
    if (bucket && !marks.has(bucket)) {
      marks.add(bucket);
      trackSafe('scroll_depth', { ...ctx(), percent: bucket });
    }
  });
})();


  // match_impression tracking disabled: triggers too often.

})();
</script>

<script>
(function() {

  var API_KEY = 'dfa4355b72741f982bcc48b15bb78ebf';
  var SRC = 'https://cdn.eu.amplitude.com/script/dfa4355b72741f982bcc48b15bb78ebf.js';

  function loadAmplitude() {
    if (document.querySelector('script[data-amp-loader]')) return;

    var tag = document.createElement('script');
    tag.src = SRC;
    tag.async = true;
    tag.setAttribute('data-amp-loader', '1');

    tag.onload = function () {
      try {
        window.amplitude.init(API_KEY, {
          serverZone: 'EU',
          fetchRemoteConfig: true,
          autocapture: true
        });
        window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('amplitude:ready'));
      } catch (e) {}
    };

    document.body.appendChild(tag);
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', function () {
    if (window.requestAnimationFrame) {
      requestAnimationFrame(loadAmplitude);
    } else {
      loadAmplitude();
    }
  });

})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
